observations.\\n311: \\tobservations, statsFunc := makeSignalObservations(logger, summary)\\n312: \\tdebugLogObservations(logger, \\\"observations\\\", observations)\\n313: \\n314: \\t// determine the PodCleanedUpFunc, monitoringInterval time.Duration) {\n189: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n190: \tthresholdHandler := func(message string) {\n191: \t\tlogger.Info(message)\n192: \t\t_, _ = \n246: // synchronize is the main control loop that enforces eviction thresholds.\n247: // Returns the pod that was killed, or nil if no pod was killed.\n248: func (m *managerImpl) synchronize(ctx context.Context, diskInfoProvider DiskInfoProvider, podFunc ActivePodsFunc) ([]*v1.Pod, error) {\n249: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n250: \t// if we have nothing to do, just return\n251: \tthresholds := m.config.Thresholds\n252: \tif len(thresholds) == 0 && !m.localStorageCapacityIsolation {\n253: \t\treturn nil, nil\n254: \t}\n255: \n256: \tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Eviction manager: synchronize housekeeping\")\n257: \t// build the ranking functions (if not yet known)\n258: \t// TODO: have a function in cadvisor that lets us know if global housekeeping has completed\n259: \tif m.dedicatedImageFs == nil {\n260: \t\thasImageFs, imageFsErr := diskInfoProvider.HasDedicatedImageFs(ctx)\n261: \t\tif imageFsErr != nil {\n262: \t\t\t// TODO: This should be refactored to log an error and retry the HasDedicatedImageFs\n263: \t\t\t// If we have a transient error this will never be retried and we will not set eviction signals\n264: \t\t\tlogger.Error(imageFsErr, \"Eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs\")\n265: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs: %w\", imageFsErr)\n266: \t\t}\n267: \t\tm.dedicatedImageFs = &hasImageFs\n268: \t\tsplitContainerImageFs, splitErr := diskInfoProvider.HasDedicatedContainerFs(ctx)\n269: \t\tif splitErr != nil {\n270: \t\t\t// A common error case is when there is no split filesystem\n271: \t\t\t// there is an error finding the split filesystem label and we want to ignore these errors\n272: \t\t\tlogger.Error(splitErr, \"eviction manager: failed to check if we have separate container filesystem. Ignoring.\")\n273: \t\t}\n274: \n275: \t\t// If we are a split filesystem but the feature is turned off\n276: \t\t// we should return an error.\n277: \t\t// This is a bad state.\n278: \t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.KubeletSeparateDiskGC) && splitContainerImageFs {\n279: \t\t\tsplitDiskError := fmt.Errorf(\"KubeletSeparateDiskGC is turned off but we still have a split filesystem\")\n280: \t\t\treturn nil, splitDiskError\n281: \t\t}\n282: \t\tthresholds, err := UpdateContainerFsThresholds(m.config.Thresholds, hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n283: \t\tm.config.Thresholds = thresholds\n284: \t\tif err != nil {\n285: \t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"eviction manager: found conflicting containerfs eviction. Ignoring.\")\n286: \t\t}\n287: \t\tm.splitContainerImageFs = &splitContainerImageFs\n288: \t\tm.signalToRankFunc = buildSignalToRankFunc(hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n289: \t\tm.signalToNodeReclaimFuncs = buildSignalToNodeReclaimFuncs(m.imageGC, m.containerGC, hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n290: \t}\n291: \n292: \tlogger.V(3).Info(\"FileSystem detection\", \"DedicatedImageFs\", m.dedicatedImageFs, \"SplitImageFs\", m.splitContainerImageFs)\n293: \tactivePods := podFunc()\n294: \tupdateStats := true\n295: \tsummary, err := m.summaryProvider.Get(ctx, updateStats)\n296: \tif err != nil {\n297: \t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Eviction manager: failed to get summary stats\")\n298: \t\treturn nil, nil\n299: \t}\n300: \n301: \tif m.clock.Since(m.thresholdsLastUpdated) > notifierRefreshInterval {\n302: \t\tm.thresholdsLastUpdated = m.clock.Now()\n303: \t\tfor _, notifier := range m.thresholdNotifiers {\n304: \t\t\tif err := notifier.UpdateThreshold(ctx, summary); err != nil {\n305: \t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Eviction manager: failed to update notifier\", \"notifier\", notifier.Description(), \"err\", err)\n306: \t\t\t}\n307: \t\t}\n308: \t}\n309: \n310: \t// make observations and get a function to derive pod usage stats relative to those observations.\n311: \tobservations, statsFunc := makeSignalObservations(logger, summary)\n312: \tdebugLogObservations(logger, \"observations\", observations)\n313: \n314: \t// determine the set of thresholds met independent of grace period\n315: \tthresholds = thresholdsMet(logger, thresholds, observations, false)\n316: \tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(logger, \"thresholds - ignoring grace period\", thresholds, observations)\n317: \n318: \t// determine the set of thresholds previously met that have not yet satisfied the associated min-reclaim\n319: \tif len(m.thresholdsMet) > 0 {\n320: \t\tthresholdsNotYetResolved := thresholdsMet(logger, m.thresholdsMet, observations, true)\n321: \t\tthresholds = mergeThresholds(thresholds, thresholdsNotYetResolved)\n322: \t}\n323: \tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(logger, \"thresholds - reclaim not satisfied\", thresholds, observations)\n324: \n325: \t// track when a threshold was first observed\n326: \tnow := m.clock.Now()\n327: \tthresholdsFirstObservedAt := thresholdsFirstObservedAt(thresholds, m.thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\n328: \n329: \t// the set of node conditions that are triggered by currently observed thresholds\n330: \tnodeConditions := nodeConditions(thresholds)\n331: \tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\n332: \t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Eviction manager: node conditions - observed\", \"nodeCondition\", nodeConditions)\n333: \t}\n334: \n335: \t// track when a node condition was last observed\n336: \tnodeConditionsLastObservedAt := nodeConditionsLastObservedAt(nodeConditions, m.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, now)\n337: \n338: \t// node conditions report true if it has been observed within the transition period window\n339: \tnodeConditions = nodeConditionsObservedSince(nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, m.config.PressureTransitionPeriod, now)\n340: \tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\n341: \t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Eviction manager: node conditions - transition period not met\", \"nodeCondition\", nodeConditions)\n342: \t}\n343: \n344: \t//
